the frontmatter instead of manual string concatenation.\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe current code manually constructs YAML with f-strings, which is fragile and doesn't handle escaping. Since \u003ccode\u003eruamel.yaml\u003c/code\u003e is already a dependency (used in \u003ccode\u003e_load_markdown_format()\u003c/code\u003e), it should also be used for writing:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"from ruamel.yaml import YAML\nfrom io import StringIO\n\ndef _save_to_disk(self, reference: ReferenceContent) -\u0026gt; None:\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Save reference content to disk cache as markdown with YAML frontmatter.\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    cache_path = self._get_cache_path(reference.reference_id)\n\n    # Build frontmatter dict\n    frontmatter = {\n        \u0026quot;reference_id\u0026quot;: reference.reference_id,\n    }\n    if reference.title:\n        frontmatter[\u0026quot;title\u0026quot;] = reference.title\n    if reference.authors:\n        frontmatter[\u0026quot;authors\u0026quot;] = reference.authors\n    if reference.journal:\n        frontmatter[\u0026quot;journal\u0026quot;] = reference.journal\n    if reference.year:\n        frontmatter[\u0026quot;year\u0026quot;] = reference.year\n    if reference.doi:\n        frontmatter[\u0026quot;doi\u0026quot;] = reference.doi\n    frontmatter[\u0026quot;content_type\u0026quot;] = reference.content_type\n\n    # Serialize frontmatter with ruamel.yaml\n    yaml = YAML()\n    yaml.default_flow_style = False\n    stream = StringIO()\n    yaml.dump(frontmatter, stream)\n    frontmatter_str = stream.getvalue()\n\n    # Build markdown body\n    body_lines = []\n    if reference.title:\n        body_lines.append(f\u0026quot;# {reference.title}\u0026quot;)\n        if reference.authors:\n            body_lines.append(f\u0026quot;**Authors:** {', '.join(reference.authors)}\u0026quot;)\n        if reference.journal:\n            journal_info = reference.journal\n            if reference.year:\n                journal_info += f\u0026quot; ({reference.year})\u0026quot;\n            body_lines.append(f\u0026quot;**Journal:** {journal_info}\u0026quot;)\n        if reference.doi:\n            body_lines.append(f\u0026quot;**DOI:** [{reference.doi}](https://doi.org/{reference.doi})\u0026quot;)\n        body_lines.append(\u0026quot;\u0026quot;)\n        body_lines.append(\u0026quot;## Content\u0026quot;)\n        body_lines.append(\u0026quot;\u0026quot;)\n\n    if reference.content:\n        body_lines.append(reference.content)\n\n    # Combine into final document\n    content = f\u0026quot;---\\n{frontmatter_str}---\\n\\n\u0026quot; + \u0026quot;\\n\u0026quot;.join(body_lines)\n    cache_path.write_text(content, encoding=\u0026quot;utf-8\u0026quot;)\n    logger.info(f\u0026quot;Cached {reference.reference_id} to {cache_path}\u0026quot;)\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efrom\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eruamel\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eyaml\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eYAML\u003c/span\u003e\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003efrom\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eio\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003eimport\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-v\"\u003eStringIO\u003c/span\u003e\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-k\"\u003edef\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-en\"\u003e_save_to_disk\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eself\u003c/span\u003e, \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ereference\u003c/span\u003e: \u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003eReferenceContent\u003c/span\u003e) \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e-\u0026gt;\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eNone\u003c/span\u003e:\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003e\"\"\"Save reference content to disk cache as markdown with YAML frontmatter.\"\"\"\u003c/span\u003e\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ecache_path\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003eself\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e_get_cache_path\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ereference\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003ereference_id\u003c/span\u003e)\n\n    \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003elogger\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003einfo\u003c/span\u003e(\u003cspan class=\"pl-s\"\u003ef\"Cached \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ereference\u003c/span\u003e.\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003ereference_id\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e to \u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e{\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-s1\"\u003ecache_path\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e}\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/span\u003e\"\u003c/span\u003e)\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis approach:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eUses the same YAML library for reading and writing (symmetry)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAutomatically handles all quoting/escaping edge cases\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eIs more maintainable than manual string construction\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eFollows the principle of using proper serialization libraries for structured data\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eWorkaround\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-workaround\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Workaround\" href=\"#workaround\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eUntil fixed, users can run this script to fix cached files:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;Fix YAML quoting in linkml-reference-validator cache files.\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\nimport re\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\ndef fix_cache_files(cache_dir: Path = Path(\u0026quot;references_cache\u0026quot;)):\n    if not cache_dir.exists():\n        return\n\n    for md_file in cache_dir.glob(\u0026quot;*.md\u0026quot;):\n        content = md_file.read_text(encoding=\u0026quot;utf-8\u0026quot;)\n        if not content.startswith(\u0026quot;---\u0026quot;):\n            continue\n\n        parts = content.split(\u0026quot;---\u0026quot;, 2)\n        if len(parts) \u0026lt; 3:\n            continue\n\n        frontmatter, body = parts[1], parts[2]\n        lines = frontmatter.split(\u0026quot;\\n\u0026quot;)\n        new_lines = []\n        modified = False\n\n        for line in lines:\n            if not line.strip() or line.strip().startswith(\u0026quot;-\u0026quot;):\n                new_lines.append(line)\n                continue\n\n            match = re.match(r'^(\\s*)([a-z_]+):\\s+(.+)$', line, re.IGNORECASE)\n            if match:\n                indent, key, value = match.groups()\n                needs_quoting = (\n                    ':' in value or\n                    value.startswith('[') or\n                    value.startswith('{') or\n                    value.startswith('*') or\n                    value.startswith('\u0026amp;')\n                )\n                is_quoted = value.startswith('\u0026quot;') or value.startswith(\u0026quot;'\u0026quot;)\n\n                if needs_quoting and not is_quoted:\n                    escaped = value.replace('\u0026quot;', '\\\\\u0026quot;')\n                    new_lines.append(f'{indent}{key}: \u0026quot;{escaped}\u0026quot;')\n                    modified = True\n                    continue\n\n            new_lines.append(line)\n\n        if modified:\n            new_content = f\u0026quot;---{chr(10).join(new_lines)}---{body}\u0026quot;\n            md_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\u0026quot;utf-8\u0026quot;)\n            print(f\u0026quot;Fixed: {md_file.name}\u0026quot;)\n\nif __name__ == \u0026quot;__main__\u0026quot;:\n Bug Report: YAML Frontmatter Not Properly Quoted in Cached Markdown Files","","## Summary","","The `linkml-reference-validator` fails to parse cached reference files when the YAML frontmatter contains unquoted values with special characters (colons, square brackets, etc.).","","## Affected Component","","`linkml_reference_validator/etl/reference_fetcher.py` - specifically `_save_to_disk()` and `_load_markdown_format()` methods.","","## Description","","When `ReferenceFetcher._save_to_disk()` writes reference metadata to a markdown file with YAML frontmatter, it does not quote values that contain YAML special characters. When the same file is later read by `_load_from_disk()` -\u003e `_load_markdown_format()`, the YAML parser fails.","","### Root Cause","","In `_save_to_disk()` (lines 337-383), values are written directly without quoting:","","```python","lines.append(f\"title: {reference.title}\")","```","","If `reference.title` contains a colon (e.g., `\"Exercise-induced asthma: an overview\"`) or starts with a bracket (e.g., `\"[Differentiation of dyspnea in patients...]\"`), the resulting YAML is invalid.","","### Failing YAML Examples","","**Colon in value:**","```yaml","---","reference_id: PMID:11678516","title: Exercise-induced asthma: an overview.","---","```","The second colon in the title is interpreted as a YAML mapping separator.","","**Square bracket at start:**","```yaml","---","reference_id: PMID:29601558","title: [Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].","---","```","The `[...]` is interpreted as a YAML list.","","## Reproduction Steps","","1. Install linkml-reference-validator","2. Create a test schema with reference validation enabled:","","```yaml","# test_schema.yaml","id: https://example.org/test","name: test","prefixes:","  linkml: https://w3id.org/linkml/","  PMID: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/","","imports:","  - linkml:types","","classes:","  TestClass:","    attributes:","      reference:","        range: string","        implements:","          - linkml:authoritative_reference","      snippet:","        range: string","        implements:","          - linkml:excerpt","```","","3. Create test data referencing a paper with special characters in title:","","```yaml","# test_data.yaml","reference: \"PMID:11678516\"","snippet: \"Asthmatic attack in exercise-induced asthma is brought about by hyperventilation\"","```","","4. Run validation twice:","","```bash","# First run - fetches and caches (succeeds)","linkml-reference-validator validate data test_data.yaml --schema test_schema.yaml --target-class TestClass","","# Second run - reads from cache (FAILS)","linkml-reference-validator validate data test_data.yaml --schema test_schema.yaml --target-class TestClass","```","","## Error Message","","```","ScannerError: mapping values are not allowed in this context","  in \"\u003cunicode string\u003e\", line 3, column 31","```","","or","","```","ParserError: while parsing a block mapping","  in \"\u003cunicode string\u003e\", line 2, column 1","did not find expected key","  in \"\u003cunicode string\u003e\", line 3, column 81","```","","## Test Cases","","### Test Case 1: Title with colon","","**PMID:** 11678516","**Title:** \"Exercise-induced asthma: an overview.\"","","**Current (broken) cache format:**","```yaml","---","reference_id: PMID:11678516","title: Exercise-induced asthma: an overview.","---","```","","**Expected (fixed) cache format:**","```yaml","---","reference_id: \"PMID:11678516\"","title: \"Exercise-induced asthma: an overview.\"","---","```","","### Test Case 2: Title with square brackets","","**PMID:** 29601558","**Title:** \"[Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].\"","","**Current (broken) cache format:**","```yaml","---","reference_id: PMID:29601558","title: [Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].","---","```","","**Expected (fixed) cache format:**","```yaml","---","reference_id: \"PMID:29601558\"","title: \"[Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].\"","---","```","","### Test Case 3: DOI with special characters","","**PMID:** 11678516","**DOI:** 10.1097/00000441-200110000-00009","","**Current format (may be problematic):**","```yaml","doi: 10.1097/00000441-200110000-00009","```","","**Safer format:**","```yaml","doi: \"10.1097/00000441-200110000-00009\"","```","","## Suggested Fix","","**Use a proper YAML library to serialize the frontmatter instead of manual string concatenation.**","","The current code manually constructs YAML with f-strings, which is fragile and doesn't handle escaping. Since `ruamel.yaml` is already a dependency (used in `_load_markdown_format()`), it should also be used for writing:","","```python","from ruamel.yaml import YAML","from io import StringIO","","def _save_to_disk(self, reference: ReferenceContent) -\u003e None:","    \"\"\"Save reference content to disk cache as markdown with YAML frontmatter.\"\"\"","    cache_path = self._get_cache_path(reference.reference_id)","","    # Build frontmatter dict","    frontmatter = {","        \"reference_id\": reference.reference_id,","    }","    if reference.title:","        frontmatter[\"title\"] = reference.title","    if reference.authors:","        frontmatter[\"authors\"] = reference.authors","    if reference.journal:","        frontmatter[\"journal\"] = reference.journal","    if reference.year:","        frontmatter[\"year\"] = reference.year","    if reference.doi:","        frontmatter[\"doi\"] = reference.doi","    frontmatter[\"content_type\"] = reference.content_type","","    # Serialize frontmatter with ruamel.yaml","    yaml = YAML()","    yaml.default_flow_style = False","    stream = StringIO()","    yaml.dump(frontmatter, stream)","    frontmatter_str = stream.getvalue()","","    # Build markdown body","    body_lines = []","    if reference.title:","        body_lines.append(f\"# {reference.title}\")","        if reference.authors:","            body_lines.append(f\"**Authors:** {', '.join(reference.authors)}\")","        if reference.journal:","            journal_info = reference.journal","            if reference.year:","                journal_info += f\" ({reference.year})\"","            body_lines.append(f\"**Journal:** {journal_info}\")","        if reference.doi:","            body_lines.append(f\"**DOI:** [{reference.doi}](https://doi.org/{reference.doi})\")","        body_lines.append(\"\")","        body_lines.append(\"## Content\")","        body_lines.append(\"\")","","    if reference.content:","        body_lines.append(reference.content)","","    # Combine into final document","    content = f\"---\\n{frontmatter_str}---\\n\\n\" + \"\\n\".join(body_lines)","    cache_path.write_text(content, encoding=\"utf-8\")","    logger.info(f\"Cached {reference.reference_id} to {cache_path}\")","```","","This approach:","1. Uses the same YAML library for reading and writing (symmetry)","2. Automatically handles all quoting/escaping edge cases","3. Is more maintainable than manual string construction","4. Follows the principle of using proper serialization libraries for structured data","","## Workaround","","Until fixed, users can run this script to fix cached files:","","```python","#!/usr/bin/env python3","\"\"\"Fix YAML quoting in linkml-reference-validator cache files.\"\"\"","import re","from pathlib import Path","","def fix_cache_files(cache_dir: Path = Path(\"references_cache\")):","    if not cache_dir.exists():","        return","","    for md_file in cache_dir.glob(\"*.md\"):","        content = md_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")","        if not content.startswith(\"---\"):","            continue","","        parts = content.split(\"---\", 2)","        if len(parts) \u003c 3:","            continue","","        frontmatter, body = parts[1], parts[2]","        lines = frontmatter.split(\"\\n\")","        new_lines = []","        modified = False","","        for line in lines:","            if not line.strip() or line.strip().startswith(\"-\"):","                new_lines.append(line)","                continue","","            match = re.match(r'^(\\s*)([a-z_]+):\\s+(.+)$', line, re.IGNORECASE)","            if match:","                indent, key, value = match.groups()","                needs_quoting = (","                    ':' in value or","                    value.startswith('[') or","                    value.startswith('{') or","                    value.startswith('*') or","                    value.startswith('\u0026')","                )","                is_quoted = value.startswith('\"') or value.startswith(\"'\")","","                if needs_quoting and not is_quoted:","                    escaped = value.replace('\"', '\\\\\"')","                    new_lines.append(f'{indent}{key}: \"{escaped}\"')","                    modified = True","                    continue","","            new_lines.append(line)","","        if modified:","            new_content = f\"---{chr(10).join(new_lines)}---{body}\"","            md_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=\"utf-8\")","            print(f\"Fixed: {md_file.name}\")","","if __name__ == \"__main__\":","    fix_cache_files()","```","","## Environment","","- Python: 3.10+","- linkml-reference-validator: (installed from git main branch)","- ruamel.yaml: (dependency of linkml-reference-validator)","","## Impact","","This bug prevents validation from working on any dataset that references papers with special characters in their titles - which is extremely common in scientific literature (e.g., \"X: a study of Y\", \"[Article in French]\", etc.).","","In testing with a real knowledge base of 55 disorders, 99 out of ~150 cached reference files had this class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Bug Report: YAML Frontmatter Not Properly Quoted in Cached Markdown Files</h1><a id="user-content-bug-report-yaml-frontmatter-not-properly-quoted-in-cached-markdown-files" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Bug Report: YAML Frontmatter Not Properly Quoted in Cached Markdown Files" href="#bug-report-yaml-frontmatter-not-properly-quoted-in-cached-markdown-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Summary</h2><a id="user-content-summary" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Summary" href="#summary"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>linkml-reference-validator</code> fails to parse cached reference files when the YAML frontmatter contains unquoted values with special characters (colons, square brackets, etc.).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Affected Component</h2><a id="user-content-affected-component" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Affected Component" href="#affected-component"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><code>linkml_reference_validator/etl/reference_fetcher.py</code> - specifically <code>_save_to_disk()</code> and <code>_load_markdown_format()</code> methods.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Description</h2><a id="user-content-description" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Description" href="#description"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When <code>ReferenceFetcher._save_to_disk()</code> writes reference metadata to a markdown file with YAML frontmatter, it does not quote values that contain YAML special characters. When the same file is later read by <code>_load_from_disk()</code> -&gt; <code>_load_markdown_format()</code>, the YAML parser fails.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Root Cause</h3><a id="user-content-root-cause" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Root Cause" href="#root-cause"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In <code>_save_to_disk()</code> (lines 337-383), values are written directly without quoting:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="lines.append(f&quot;title: {reference.title}&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-s1">lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"title: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">title</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If <code>reference.title</code> contains a colon (e.g., <code>"Exercise-induced asthma: an overview"</code>) or starts with a bracket (e.g., <code>"[Differentiation of dyspnea in patients...]"</code>), the resulting YAML is invalid.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Failing YAML Examples</h3><a id="user-content-failing-yaml-examples" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Failing YAML Examples" href="#failing-yaml-examples"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Colon in value:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
reference_id: PMID:11678516
title: Exercise-induced asthma: an overview.
---"><pre>---
<span class="pl-ent">reference_id</span>: <span class="pl-s">PMID:11678516</span>
<span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">Exercise-induced asthma: an overview.</span>
---</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The second colon in the title is interpreted as a YAML mapping separator.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Square bracket at start:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
reference_id: PMID:29601558
title: [Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].
---"><pre>---
<span class="pl-ent">reference_id</span>: <span class="pl-s">PMID:29601558</span>
<span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">[Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].</span>
---</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>[...]</code> is interpreted as a YAML list.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Reproduction Steps</h2><a id="user-content-reproduction-steps" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Reproduction Steps" href="#reproduction-steps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Install linkml-reference-validator</li>
<li>Create a test schema with reference validation enabled:</li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# test_schema.yaml
id: https://example.org/test
name: test
prefixes:
  linkml: https://w3id.org/linkml/
  PMID: https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/

imports:
  - linkml:types

classes:
  TestClass:
    attributes:
      reference:
        range: string
        implements:
          - linkml:authoritative_reference
      snippet:
        range: string
        implements:
          - linkml:excerpt"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> test_schema.yaml</span>
<span class="pl-ent">id</span>: <span class="pl-s">https://example.org/test</span>
<span class="pl-ent">name</span>: <span class="pl-s">test</span>
<span class="pl-ent">prefixes</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">linkml</span>: <span class="pl-s">https://w3id.org/linkml/</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">PMID</span>: <span class="pl-s">https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/</span>

<span class="pl-ent">imports</span>:
  - <span class="pl-s">linkml:types</span>

<span class="pl-ent">classes</span>:
  <span class="pl-ent">TestClass</span>:
    <span class="pl-ent">attributes</span>:
      <span class="pl-ent">reference</span>:
        <span class="pl-ent">range</span>: <span class="pl-s">string</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">implements</span>:
          - <span class="pl-s">linkml:authoritative_reference</span>
      <span class="pl-ent">snippet</span>:
        <span class="pl-ent">range</span>: <span class="pl-s">string</span>
        <span class="pl-ent">implements</span>:
          - <span class="pl-s">linkml:excerpt</span></pre></div>
<ol start="3" dir="auto">
<li>Create test data referencing a paper with special characters in title:</li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# test_data.yaml
reference: &quot;PMID:11678516&quot;
snippet: &quot;Asthmatic attack in exercise-induced asthma is brought about by hyperventilation&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> test_data.yaml</span>
<span class="pl-ent">reference</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>PMID:11678516<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-ent">snippet</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Asthmatic attack in exercise-induced asthma is brought about by hyperventilation<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<ol start="4" dir="auto">
<li>Run validation twice:</li>
</ol>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# First run - fetches and caches (succeeds)
linkml-reference-validator validate data test_data.yaml --schema test_schema.yaml --target-class TestClass

# Second run - reads from cache (FAILS)
linkml-reference-validator validate data test_data.yaml --schema test_schema.yaml --target-class TestClass"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> First run - fetches and caches (succeeds)</span>
linkml-reference-validator validate data test_data.yaml --schema test_schema.yaml --target-class TestClass

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Second run - reads from cache (FAILS)</span>
linkml-reference-validator validate data test_data.yaml --schema test_schema.yaml --target-class TestClass</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Error Message</h2><a id="user-content-error-message" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Error Message" href="#error-message"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Test Cases</h2><a id="user-content-test-cases" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Test Cases" href="#test-cases"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Test Case 1: Title with colon</h3><a id="user-content-test-case-1-title-with-colon" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Test Case 1: Title with colon" href="#test-case-1-title-with-colon"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>PMID:</strong> 11678516
<strong>Title:</strong> "Exercise-induced asthma: an overview."</p>

title: Exercise-induced asthma: an overview.

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Test Case 2: Title with square brackets</h3><a id="user-content-test-case-2-title-with-square-brackets" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Test Case 2: Title with square brackets" href="#test-case-2-title-with-square-brackets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>PMID:</strong> 29601558
<strong>Title:</strong> "[Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis]."</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Current (broken) cache format:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
reference_id: PMID:29601558
title: [Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].
---"><pre>---
<span class="pl-ent">reference_id</span>: <span class="pl-s">PMID:29601558</span>
<span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s">[Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].</span>
---</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Expected (fixed) cache format:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="---
reference_id: &quot;PMID:29601558&quot;
title: &quot;[Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].&quot;
---"><pre>---
<span class="pl-ent">reference_id</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>PMID:29601558<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-ent">title</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>[Differentiation of dyspnea in patients with asthma and lung sarcoidosis].<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
---</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Test Case 3: DOI with special characters</h3><a id="user-content-test-case-3-doi-with-special-characters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Test Case 3: DOI with special characters" href="#test-case-3-doi-with-special-characters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>PMID:</strong> 11678516
<strong>DOI:</strong> 10.1097/00000441-200110000-00009</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Current format (may be problematic):</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="doi: 10.1097/00000441-200110000-00009"><pre><span class="pl-ent">doi</span>: <span class="pl-s">10.1097/00000441-200110000-00009</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Safer format:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="doi: &quot;10.1097/00000441-200110000-00009&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-ent">doi</span>: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>10.1097/00000441-200110000-00009<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Suggested Fix</h2><a id="user-content-suggested-fix" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Suggested Fix" href="#suggested-fix"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Use a proper YAML library to serialize the frontmatter instead of manual string concatenation.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">The current code manually constructs YAML with f-strings, which is fragile and doesn't handle escaping. Since <code>ruamel.yaml</code> is already a dependency (used in <code>_load_markdown_format()</code>), it should also be used for writing:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from ruamel.yaml import YAML
from io import StringIO

def _save_to_disk(self, reference: ReferenceContent) -&gt; None:
    &quot;&quot;&quot;Save reference content to disk cache as markdown with YAML frontmatter.&quot;&quot;&quot;
    cache_path = self._get_cache_path(reference.reference_id)

    # Build frontmatter dict
    frontmatter = {
        &quot;reference_id&quot;: reference.reference_id,
    }
    if reference.title:
        frontmatter[&quot;title&quot;] = reference.title
    if reference.authors:
        frontmatter[&quot;authors&quot;] = reference.authors
    if reference.journal:
        frontmatter[&quot;journal&quot;] = reference.journal
    if reference.year:
        frontmatter[&quot;year&quot;] = reference.year
    if reference.doi:
        frontmatter[&quot;doi&quot;] = reference.doi
    frontmatter[&quot;content_type&quot;] = reference.content_type

    # Serialize frontmatter with ruamel.yaml
    yaml = YAML()
    yaml.default_flow_style = False
    stream = StringIO()
    yaml.dump(frontmatter, stream)
    frontmatter_str = stream.getvalue()

    # Build markdown body
    body_lines = []
    if reference.title:
        body_lines.append(f&quot;# {reference.title}&quot;)
        if reference.authors:
            body_lines.append(f&quot;**Authors:** {', '.join(reference.authors)}&quot;)
        if reference.journal:
            journal_info = reference.journal
            if reference.year:
                journal_info += f&quot; ({reference.year})&quot;
            body_lines.append(f&quot;**Journal:** {journal_info}&quot;)
        if reference.doi:
            body_lines.append(f&quot;**DOI:** [{reference.doi}](https://doi.org/{reference.doi})&quot;)
        body_lines.append(&quot;&quot;)
        body_lines.append(&quot;## Content&quot;)
        body_lines.append(&quot;&quot;)

    if reference.content:
        body_lines.append(reference.content)

    # Combine into final document
    content = f&quot;---\n{frontmatter_str}---\n\n&quot; + &quot;\n&quot;.join(body_lines)
    cache_path.write_text(content, encoding=&quot;utf-8&quot;)
    logger.info(f&quot;Cached {reference.reference_id} to {cache_path}&quot;)"><pre><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">ruamel</span>.<span class="pl-s1">yaml</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-c1">YAML</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">io</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">StringIO</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">_save_to_disk</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>: <span class="pl-smi">ReferenceContent</span>) <span class="pl-c1">-&gt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>:
    <span class="pl-s">"""Save reference content to disk cache as markdown with YAML frontmatter."""</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">cache_path</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">_get_cache_path</span>(<span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">reference_id</span>)

    <span class="pl-c"># Build frontmatter dict</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> {
        <span class="pl-s">"reference_id"</span>: <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">reference_id</span>,
    }
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">title</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span>[<span class="pl-s">"title"</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">title</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">authors</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span>[<span class="pl-s">"authors"</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">authors</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">journal</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span>[<span class="pl-s">"journal"</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">journal</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">year</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span>[<span class="pl-s">"year"</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">year</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">doi</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span>[<span class="pl-s">"doi"</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">doi</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span>[<span class="pl-s">"content_type"</span>] <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">content_type</span>

    <span class="pl-c"># Serialize frontmatter with ruamel.yaml</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">yaml</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">YAML</span>()
    <span class="pl-s1">yaml</span>.<span class="pl-c1">default_flow_style</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">False</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">stream</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">StringIO</span>()
    <span class="pl-s1">yaml</span>.<span class="pl-c1">dump</span>(<span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span>, <span class="pl-s1">stream</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter_str</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">stream</span>.<span class="pl-c1">getvalue</span>()

    <span class="pl-c"># Build markdown body</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">title</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"# <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">title</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">authors</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"**Authors:** <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s">', '</span>.<span class="pl-c1">join</span>(<span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">authors</span>)<span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">journal</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">journal_info</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">journal</span>
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">year</span>:
                <span class="pl-s1">journal_info</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s">f" (<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">year</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>)"</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"**Journal:** <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">journal_info</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">doi</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"**DOI:** [<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">doi</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>](https://doi.org/<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">doi</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>)"</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s">""</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s">"## Content"</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s">""</span>)

    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">content</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">content</span>)

    <span class="pl-c"># Combine into final document</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">content</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">f"---<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">frontmatter_str</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>---<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-cce">\n</span>"</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s">"<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>"</span>.<span class="pl-c1">join</span>(<span class="pl-s1">body_lines</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">cache_path</span>.<span class="pl-c1">write_text</span>(<span class="pl-s1">content</span>, <span class="pl-s1">encoding</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"utf-8"</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">logger</span>.<span class="pl-c1">info</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"Cached <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">reference</span>.<span class="pl-c1">reference_id</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span> to <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">cache_path</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">This approach:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Uses the same YAML library for reading and writing (symmetry)</li>
<li>Automatically handles all quoting/escaping edge cases</li>
<li>Is more maintainable than manual string construction</li>
<li>Follows the principle of using proper serialization libraries for structured data</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Workaround</h2><a id="user-content-workaround" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Workaround" href="#workaround"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Until fixed, users can run this script to fix cached files:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#!/usr/bin/env python3
&quot;&quot;&quot;Fix YAML quoting in linkml-reference-validator cache files.&quot;&quot;&quot;
import re
from pathlib import Path

def fix_cache_files(cache_dir: Path = Path(&quot;references_cache&quot;)):
    if not cache_dir.exists():
        return

    for md_file in cache_dir.glob(&quot;*.md&quot;):
        content = md_file.read_text(encoding=&quot;utf-8&quot;)
        if not content.startswith(&quot;---&quot;):
            continue

        parts = content.split(&quot;---&quot;, 2)
        if len(parts) &lt; 3:
            continue

        frontmatter, body = parts[1], parts[2]
        lines = frontmatter.split(&quot;\n&quot;)
        new_lines = []
        modified = False

        for line in lines:
            if not line.strip() or line.strip().startswith(&quot;-&quot;):
                new_lines.append(line)
                continue

            match = re.match(r'^(\s*)([a-z_]+):\s+(.+)$', line, re.IGNORECASE)
            if match:
                indent, key, value = match.groups()
                needs_quoting = (
                    ':' in value or
                    value.startswith('[') or
                    value.startswith('{') or
                    value.startswith('*') or
                    value.startswith('&amp;')
                )
                is_quoted = value.startswith('&quot;') or value.startswith(&quot;'&quot;)

                if needs_quoting and not is_quoted:
                    escaped = value.replace('&quot;', '\\&quot;')
                    new_lines.append(f'{indent}{key}: &quot;{escaped}&quot;')
                    modified = True
                    continue

            new_lines.append(line)

        if modified:
            new_content = f&quot;---{chr(10).join(new_lines)}---{body}&quot;
            md_file.write_text(new_content, encoding=&quot;utf-8&quot;)
            print(f&quot;Fixed: {md_file.name}&quot;)

if __name__ == &quot;__main__&quot;:
    fix_cache_files()"><pre><span class="pl-c">#!/usr/bin/env python3</span>
<span class="pl-s">"""Fix YAML quoting in linkml-reference-validator cache files."""</span>
<span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-s1">re</span>
<span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">pathlib</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">Path</span>

<span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">fix_cache_files</span>(<span class="pl-s1">cache_dir</span>: <span class="pl-smi">Path</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">Path</span>(<span class="pl-s">"references_cache"</span>)):
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-c1">not</span> <span class="pl-s1">cache_dir</span>.<span class="pl-c1">exists</span>():
        <span class="pl-k">return</span>

    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">md_file</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">cache_dir</span>.<span class="pl-c1">glob</span>(<span class="pl-s">"*.md"</span>):
        <span class="pl-s1">content</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">md_file</span>.<span class="pl-c1">read_text</span>(<span class="pl-s1">encoding</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"utf-8"</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-c1">not</span> <span class="pl-s1">content</span>.<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s">"---"</span>):
            <span class="pl-k">continue</span>

        <span class="pl-s1">parts</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">content</span>.<span class="pl-c1">split</span>(<span class="pl-s">"---"</span>, <span class="pl-c1">2</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">parts</span>) <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">3</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">continue</span>

        <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span>, <span class="pl-s1">body</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">parts</span>[<span class="pl-c1">1</span>], <span class="pl-s1">parts</span>[<span class="pl-c1">2</span>]
        <span class="pl-s1">lines</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">frontmatter</span>.<span class="pl-c1">split</span>(<span class="pl-s">"<span class="pl-cce">\n</span>"</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">new_lines</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
        <span class="pl-s1">modified</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">False</span>

        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">line</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">lines</span>:
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-c1">not</span> <span class="pl-s1">line</span>.<span class="pl-c1">strip</span>() <span class="pl-c1">or</span> <span class="pl-s1">line</span>.<span class="pl-c1">strip</span>().<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s">"-"</span>):
                <span class="pl-s1">new_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s1">line</span>)
                <span class="pl-k">continue</span>

            <span class="pl-s1">match</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">re</span>.<span class="pl-c1">match</span>(<span class="pl-s">r'^(\s*)([a-z_]+):\s+(.+)$'</span>, <span class="pl-s1">line</span>, <span class="pl-s1">re</span>.<span class="pl-c1">IGNORECASE</span>)
            <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">match</span>:
                <span class="pl-s1">indent</span>, <span class="pl-s1">key</span>, <span class="pl-s1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">match</span>.<span class="pl-c1">groups</span>()
                <span class="pl-s1">needs_quoting</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (
                    <span class="pl-s">':'</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span> <span class="pl-c1">or</span>
                    <span class="pl-s1">value</span>.<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s">'['</span>) <span class="pl-c1">or</span>
                    <span class="pl-s1">value</span>.<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s">'{'</span>) <span class="pl-c1">or</span>
                    <span class="pl-s1">value</span>.<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s">'*'</span>) <span class="pl-c1">or</span>
                    <span class="pl-s1">value</span>.<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s">'&amp;'</span>)
                )
                <span class="pl-s1">is_quoted</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span>.<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s">'"'</span>) <span class="pl-c1">or</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span>.<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s">"'"</span>)

                <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">needs_quoting</span> <span class="pl-c1">and</span> <span class="pl-c1">not</span> <span class="pl-s1">is_quoted</span>:
                    <span class="pl-s1">escaped</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">value</span>.<span class="pl-c1">replace</span>(<span class="pl-s">'"'</span>, <span class="pl-s">'<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>"'</span>)
                    <span class="pl-s1">new_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s">f'<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">indent</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span><span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">key</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>: "<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">escaped</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"'</span>)
                    <span class="pl-s1">modified</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">True</span>
                    <span class="pl-k">continue</span>

            <span class="pl-s1">new_lines</span>.<span class="pl-c1">append</span>(<span class="pl-s1">line</span>)

        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">modified</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">new_content</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s">f"---<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-en">chr</span>(<span class="pl-c1">10</span>).<span class="pl-c1">join</span>(<span class="pl-s1">new_lines</span>)<span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>---<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">body</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">md_file</span>.<span class="pl-c1">write_text</span>(<span class="pl-s1">new_content</span>, <span class="pl-s1">encoding</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">"utf-8"</span>)
            <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"Fixed: <span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">md_file</span>.<span class="pl-c1">name</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>"</span>)

<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">__name__</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-s">"__main__"</span>:
    <span class="pl-en">fix_cache_files</span>()</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Environment</h2><a id="user-content-environment" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Environment" href="#environment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Python: 3.10+</li>
<li>linkml-reference-validator: (installed from git main branch)</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Impact</h2><a id="user-content-impact" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Impact" href="#impact"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This bug prevents validation from working on any dataset that references papers with special characters in their titles - which is extremely common in scientific literature (e.g., "X: a study of Y", "[Article in French]", etc.).</p>
<p dir="auto">In testing with a real knowledge base of 55 disorders, 99 out of ~150 cached reference files had this issue.</p>
